)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@IR
)@@G@@   . THE WRAPUP ROUTINE.  IF WE     @G@@@@          TG,U      A1,PIPSTOPIS
)@@G@@         . DID, WE DON'T DARE BYPASS IT   @H@@@@          J         $+2 IT
)@@G@@               . OR THE WRAPPING UP MIGHT NOT WORK    @G@@@@          J IU
)@@G@@        CONT               . FROM WRAPUP, SO RETURN NOW     @D@@@@      IV
)@@G@@    TZ        NEWABS            . NEW ABSOLUTE  @E@@@@          J       IW
)@@G@@  NEW               . YES, GET DESCRIPTOR @E@@@@          L,U       A0,4IX
)@@G@@              . NO BUILD DESCRIPTOR @B@@@@          TG,U      A1,FRSTD$ IY
)@@G@@       .    @B@@@@          L,U       A0,5              .   @B@@@@      IZ
)@@G@@    S         A0,CPKT+1         .   @B@@@@          J         BOTH      JA
)@@G@@        .   @]@@@@NEW       . @D@@@@          L         A0,CPKT+1       JB
)@@G@@  . GET BANK$     @D@@@@          SSC       A0,12             . PACK INTJC
)@@G@@O HALF@B@@@@          SSL       A0,24             .   @]@@@@BOTH      . JD
)@@G@@@F@@@@          S         A0,BANK           . REMEMBER THE BANK INDEX   JE
)@@G@@@B@@@@          S         A1,A1SAVEC        .   @B@@@@          DS      JF
)@@G@@  A2,A2SAVE         .   @D@@@@          DS        A4,A4SAVE         . SAJG
)@@G@@VE THE REGS @B@@@@          S         R1,R1SAVE         .   @B@@@@      JH
)@@G@@    S         R2,R2SAVE         .   @B@@@@          S         R3,R3SAVE JI
)@@G@@        .   @E@@@@          LMJ       X11,USRPIP        . CALL USER OWN JJ
)@@G@@CODE  @E@@@@          +         CPKT              . PASS HIM THE PACKET JK
)@@G@@@I@@@@          +         EXTRADDR          . GET BACK THE ADDRESS OF THJL
)@@G@@E EXTRA VECTOR    @F@@@@          +         (0100,WBK$)       . BE NICE JM
)@@G@@IN CASE IT FORTRAN@B@@@@          L         A1,A1SAVEC        .   @B@@@@JN
)@@G@@          DL        A2,A2SAVE         .   @E@@@@          DL        A4,AJO
)@@G@@4SAVE         . RELOAD THE REGS     @B@@@@          L         R1,R1SAVE JP
)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@          L         R2,R2SAVE         .   @B@@@@      JQ
)@@G@@    L         R3,R3SAVE         .   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          TNZ,U   JR
)@@G@@  SLT$              . IS THIS PROGRAM SEGMENTED @F@@@@          J       JS
)@@G@@  NOSEG             . NO, THEN PROCEED QUICKLY  @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.     JT
)@@G@@    ****** SEGMENTED PROGRAMS ONLY WILL GO THRU THE FOLLOWING *****     JU
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @D@@@@          DS        A2,A2SAVE         . STORE THE REGSJV
)@@G@@@B@@@@          S         A4,A4SAVE         .   @F@@@@          L,U     JW
)@@G@@  A0,SLT$           . SET UP FOR SEARCH OF SLT$ @G@@@@          TZ,S2   JX
)@@G@@  0,A0              . IS THIS THE OLD STYLE ABSOLUTE  @G@@@@          J JY
)@@G@@        NTYPE             . NO, PERFORM MODIFIED SEARCH     @B@@@@      JZ
)@@G@@    J         NXTSEG1          .    @C@@@@NXTSEG    . OLD STYLE ABSOLUTEKA
)@@G@@ SEGMENT SEARCH   @F@@@@          A,U       A0,SLT$           . MAKE ADDKB
)@@G@@RESS ABSOLUTE     @]@@@@NXTSEG1   . @G@@@@          L         A3,1,A0   KC
)@@G@@        . GET ADDRESS LIMITS FOR IBANK    @F@@@@          TG,U      A1,FKD
)@@G@@RSTD$         . THIS IS IBANK, ISN'T IT   @G@@@@          L         A3,2KE
)@@G@@,A0           . NO, GET ADDRESS LIMITS FOR DBANK@D@@@@          L,U     KF
)@@G@@  A4,0              . CLEAR  UPPER  @F@@@@          LDSC      A3,18     KG
)@@G@@        . SET LOWER AND UPPER LIMITS@B@@@@          SSL       A3,18     KH
)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@          AN,U      A3,1              .   @G@@@@      KI
)@@G@@    TNW,U     A3,0,A1           . IS THE ADDRESS IN THIS SEGMENT  @E@@@@KJ
)@@G@@          J         GOTIT             . YES, CLEAR OUT .    @F@@@@      KK
)@@G@@    L,H2      A0,0,A0           . GET NEXT ACTIVE SEGMENT   @F@@@@      KL
)@@G@@    JNZ       A0,NXTSEG         . IF THERE IS ONE, CONTINUE @G@@@@      KM
)@@G@@    J         ERROR             . ELSE, GO RECORD THIS AS AN ERROR@[@@@@KN
)@@G@@.     @C@@@@NXTNSG   . NEW STYLE ABSOLUTE SEGMENT SEARCH    @F@@@@      KO
)@@G@@    L,H2      A0,0,A0           . GET NEXT ACTIVE SEGMENT   @H@@@@      KP
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,GOTIT0         . IF NOMORE, ASSUME THIS IS MAIN SEG    KQ
)@@G@@@F@@@@          A,U       A0,SLT$           . MAKE ADDRESS ABSOLUTE     KR
)@@G@@@A@@@@NTYPE     . NEW STYLE ABS. ENTRY    @G@@@@          L,U       A2,0KS
)@@G@@,A0           . SET UP FOR EXTENSION SEARCH     @B@@@@          J       KT
)@@G@@  NEXTEN1           .   @E@@@@NEXTEN    L,H2      A2,2,A2           . GEKU
)@@G@@T NEXT EXTENSION  @F@@@@          JZ        A2,NXTNSG         . IF NONE,KV
)@@G@@ GET NEXT SEG     @F@@@@          A,U       A2,SLT$           . MAKE ADDKW
)@@G@@RESS ABSOLUTE     @]@@@@NEXTEN1   . @D@@@@          L         A3,2,A2   KX
)@@G@@        . GET BANK INDEX@B@@@@          SSL       A3,24             .   KY
)@@G@@@F@@@@          TE        A3,BANK           . IS THIS THE BANK WE WANT  KZ
)@@G@@@D@@@@          J         NEXTEN            . NO, GET NEXT  @G@@@@      LA
)@@G@@    L,U       A4,0              . SET UPPER AND LOWER FOR TEST    @B@@@@LB
)@@G@@          L         A3,1,A2           .   @B@@@@          LDSC      A3,1LC
)@@G@@8             .   @B@@@@          SSL       A3,18             .   @B@@@@LD
)@@G@@          AN,U      A3,1              .   @G@@@@          TW,U      A3,0LE
)@@G@@,A1           . IS THIS THE CORRECT BANK AAD SEG@E@@@@          J       LF
)@@G@@  NXTNSG            . NO, GET NEXT SEGMENT@]@@@@GOTIT     . @E@@@@      LG
)@@G@@    AN,U      A0,SLT$           . COMPUTE SEGMENT     @B@@@@          SSLH
)@@G@@L       A0,2              .\  @]@@@@GOTIT0    . @H@@@@          TNE     LI
)@@G@@  A0,CURSEG         . IS THIS THE SAME SEGMENT AS LAST TIME @F@@@@      LJ
)@@G@@    J         NORITE            . YES, THEN DON'T RECORD IT @F@@@@      LK
)@@G@@    S         A0,CURSEG         . NO, SAVE IT AS THE LAST   @F@@@@      LL
)@@G@@    L         A3,POINT          . AND WRITE IT TO THE BUFFER@B@@@@      LM
)@@G@@    SN        A0,BUF,*A3        .   @B@@@@          S         A3,POINT  LN
)@@G@@        .   @F@@@@          L,U       A0,0,A3           . GET CURRENT BULO
)@@G@@FFER LOC    @E@@@@          TLE,U     A0,BUFLEN         . IS THE BUFFER LP
)@@G@@FULL  @C@@@@          J         NORITE           . NO, SKIP @B@@@@      LQ
)@@G@@    SZ        DELTIM            .   @F@@@@          L,U       A1,BUFSEC LR
)@@G@@        . SET TO WRITE FULL BUFFER  @D@@@@          LMJ       X11,WRITE LS
)@@G@@        . WRITE BUFFER  @E@@@@NORITE    DL        A2,A2SAVE         . RELT
)@@G@@LOAD REGISTERS    @B@@@@          L         A4,A4SAVE         .   @[@@@@LU
)@@G@@.     @#@@@@.         ********@[@@@@.     @]@@@@NOSEG     . @D@@@@      LV
)@@G@@    L         A0,BANK           . RELOAD BANK   @H@@@@          LSSL    LW
)@@G@@  A1,18             . COMBINE BANK AND ADDRESS INTO ONE WORD@B@@@@      LX
)@@G@@    LDSL      A0,18             .   @E@@@@          L         A1,POINT  LY
)@@G@@         . STORE WORD INTO    @G@@@@          S         A0,BUF,*A1      LZ
)@@G@@   . BUFFER AND INCREMENT POINTER   @F@@@@          S         A1,POINT  MA
)@@G@@         . REPLACE UPDATED POINTER  @E@@@@          BUMP      COUNT     MB
)@@G@@         . INCREMENT PIP COUNT@F@@@@          L,U       A0,,A1          MC
)@@G@@   . SEE IF THE BUFFER IS FULL@G@@@@          TLE,U     A0,BUFLEN       MD
)@@G@@     . AND IF IT IS, WRITE IT OUT   @B@@@@          J         EXTWRT    ME
)@@G@@           .@B@@@@          SZ        DELTIM            .   @F@@@@      MF
)@@G@@    L,U       A1,BUFSEC         . SET TO WRITE FULL BUFFER  @D@@@@      MG
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,WRITE         . WRITE BUFFER  @[@@@@.     @C@@@@.  ** MH
)@@G@@WRITE THE EXTRA VECTOR IF THERE IS ONE    @[@@@@.     @]@@@@EXTWRT    . MI
)@@G@@@E@@@@          L         A0,NXTRA          . GET LENGTH OF EXTRA @D@@@@MJ
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,CONT           . IF NONE, SKIP @F@@@@          DSMK
)@@G@@        A2,A2SAVE         . ELSE, MAKE A LITTLE ROOM  @B@@@@          S ML
)@@G@@        A4,A4SAVE         .   @D@@@@          L         A2,POINT        MM
)@@G@@  . GET INDEX     @E@@@@          LXI,U     A3,1              . SET UP EMN
)@@G@@XTRA PTR    @B@@@@          LXM       A3,EXTRADDR       .   @E@@@@      MO
)@@G@@    L         A4,A0             . GET COUNT OF WORDS  @]@@@@EXTWRT1   . MP
)@@G@@@D@@@@          JGD       A4,$+2            . ONE AT A TIME @E@@@@      MQ
)@@G@@    J         EXTWRT2           . WHEN DONE, GET OUT  @D@@@@          L MR
)@@G@@        A1,0,*A3          . GET A WORD    @D@@@@          S         A1,BMS
)@@G@@UF,*A2        . AND STORE IT  @E@@@@          L,U       A1,,A2          MT
)@@G@@  . CHECK FOR OVERFLOW  @D@@@@          TLE,U     A1,BUFLEN         . OFMU
)@@G@@ THE BUFFER @F@@@@          J         EXTWRT1           . IF NOT, KEEP OMV
)@@G@@N TRUCKIN   @E@@@@          SZ        DELTIM            .  ELSE, WE MUSTMW
)@@G@@ WRITE@D@@@@          L,U       A1,BUFSEC         . A FULL BUFFER @B@@@@MX
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,WRITE         .   @B@@@@          L         A2,PMY
)@@G@@OINT          .   @E@@@@          J         EXTWRT1           . AND DO SMZ
)@@G@@OME MORE    @#@@@@EXTWRT2   .    .  @F@@@@          S         A2,POINT  NA
)@@G@@        . KEEP TRACK OF WHERE WE ARE@B@@@@          DL        A2,A2SAVE NB
)@@G@@        .P  @B@@@@          L         A4,A4SAVE         .   @[@@@@.     NC
)@@G@@@ @@@@. **** END OF EXTRA VECTOR    @[@@@@.     @F@@@@CONT      RANDOM  ND
)@@G@@                     . GENERATE NEW TRAP REQUEST@E@@@@          DL      NE
)@@G@@  A0,SAVEC           . RESTORE REGISTERS  @B@@@@          L         X11,NF
)@@G@@SX11C         .   @H@@@@          J         *RETURN1            . AND GONG
)@@G@@ BACK TO MAINSTREAM EXECUTION @G@@@@ERROR     BUMP      ERCOUNT         NH
)@@G@@   . COUNT HOW OFTEN WE BLOW IT     @G@@@@                              NI
)@@G@@         . THEN BYPASS BOTH INTERRUPTS    @F@@@@          J         CONTNJ
)@@G@@               . BY RETURNING DIRECTLY    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@WRITE     . NK
)@@G@@WRITE BUFFER, A1 CONTAINS LENGTH    @D@@@@          L         A0,COUNT  NL
)@@G@@        . SAVE COUNT    @B@@@@          S         A0,PCOUNT         .   NM

)@@G@@@B@@@@          ER        IOW$              .   @D@@@@          L       NO
)@@G@@  A0,COUNT          . UPDATE COUNT  @B@@@@          A         A0,PCOUNT NP
)@@G@@        .   @B@@@@          S         A0,COUNT          .   @F@@@@      NQ

)@@G@@    S         A0,DRUMW+5        .   @F@@@@          A         A0,A1     NS

)@@G@@    SAXR$   @F@@@^          LIT                         . LITERALS INTO RE
)@@G@@THE IBANK   @E@C@^          TYPE      TYPE$REP          . NO IBANK STORERF
)@@G@@S     @E@@@C          $INFO     9 1               . NO IBANK STORES     RG
)@@G@@@A@@@^OP        EQU       'OLD PROGRAM'.  @^@@@^          STRUC$,OP .   RH
)@@G@@@^@@@^          ELT$      .   @[@@@^.     @#@@@^. DEBUG = 0 : CSF$@ @@@^RI
)@@G@@.       = 1 : CSF$ AND PRINT$ @ @@@^.       = 2 :          PRINT$ @[@@@^RJ
)@@G@@.     @E@ @^DEBUG     EQU       0                 . TURN OFF DEBUG CODE RK
)@@G@@@E@@@ DEBUG     EQU       0                 . TURN OFF DEBUG CODE @B@@@^RL
)@@G@@          BRIEF                       .   @B@@@^PF        FORM      12,6RM
)@@G@@,18           .   @[@@@^.     @G@@@^. THIS IS AN ATTEMPT TO REGENERATE TRN
)@@G@@HE FABLED LOST 'FCYCLE' PROCESSOR   @A@@@^. OF WHICH ONLY AN ABSOLUTE RERO
)@@G@@MAINS.@[@@@^.     @]@@@^FCYCLE    . @E@@@^          TNE,U     A4,4      RP
)@@G@@        . ARE WE DEMAND ?     @D@@@^          S         A4,DEMAND       RQ
)@@G@@  . YES - SET FLAG@[@@@^.     @E@@@^. READ IN THE INFOR ( PROCESSOR CALLRR
)@@G@@ CARD INFORMATION )     @[@@@^.     @G@@@^          LA        A0,INFRDR RS
)@@G@@        . GET ACCESS WORD TO INFOR BUFFER @D@@@^          CALL      RINFRT
)@@G@@$             . READ INFOR    @G@@@^          J         ERRPRT          RU
)@@G@@  . PRINT MESSAGE AND ERROR OFF     @[@@@^.     @ @@@^. GET USENAME FROMRV
)@@G@@ SPEC 2     @[@@@^.     @B@@@^          LA,U      A0,2              .   RW
)@@G@@@G@@@^          LA,U      A4,'I'            . A4 IS DEFAULT LOGICAL SUBSRX
)@@G@@YSTEM.@D@@@^          CALL,X9   SPEC              . GO AND DO IT  @G@@@^RY
)@@G@@          J         ERRPRT            . PRINT MESSAGE AND ERROR OFF     RZ
)@@G@@@G@@@^          DL        A0,('OLD$FILE    ') . NONE SPECIFIED , USE FILSA
)@@G@@E NAME@G@@@^          DS        A0,DREADF         . SET FILENAME FOR DRESB
)@@G@@AD FUNCTION @F@@@^          S         A3,OLDEQP         . SET OLD EQUIPMSC
)@@G@@ENT CODE    @E@@@^          S         A2,ASGOLD         . STORE FOUND FLSD
)@@G@@AG    @F@@@^          SA        A4,OLDLOG         . STASH LOGICAL SUBSYSSE
)@@G@@TEM.  @[@@@^.     @ @@@^. GET USENAME FROM SPEC 3     @[@@@^.     @B@@@^SF
)@@G@@          LA,U      A0,3              .   @G@@@^          LA,U      A4,'SG
)@@G@@O'            . A4 IS DEFAULT LOGICAL SUBSYSTEM.@D@@@^          CALL,X9 SH
)@@G@@  SPEC              . GO AND DO IT  @G@@@^          J         ERRPRT    SI
)@@G@@        . PRINT MESSAGE AND ERROR OFF     @E@@@^          DSL       A0,7SJ
)@@G@@2             . NO FIND - CLEAR REG @B@@@^          DS        A0,XXFILE SK
)@@G@@        .   @F@@@^          S         A3,NEWEQP         . SET NEW EQUIPMSL
)@@G@@ENT CODE    @E@@@^          S         A2,ASGNEW         . STORE FOUND FLSM
)@@G@@AG    @F@@@^          SA        A4,NEWLOG         . STASH LOGICAL SUBSYSSN
)@@G@@TEM.  @[@@@^.     @A@@@^. GET PERMUTATION COUNT (SPEC 4)    @[@@@^.     SO
)@@G@@@B@@@^          LA,U      A0,4              .   @C@@@^          CALL,X9 SP
)@@G@@  SPEC              . GET IT  @F@@@^          J         ERRCNT          SQ
)@@G@@  . ERROR IN PERMUTATION COUNT@D@@@^          LA        A0,('1     ')   SR
)@@G@@  . GET DEFAULT   @[@@@^/.    @[@@@^.     @B@@@^. CONVERT PERMUTATION COSS
)@@G@@UNT TO BINARY     @[@@@^.     @F@@@^          DSL       A1,72           ST
)@@G@@  . CLEAR TEMP , ACCUMULATOR  @F@@@^          DSL       A0,30           SU
)@@G@@  . ALL BUT FIRST CHAR TO A1  @F@@@^          LN,U      A6,1            SV
)@@G@@  . SET FLAG MINUS SIGN SEEN  @E@@@^          TNE,U     A0,'-'          SW
)@@G@@  . WAS COUNT NEGATIVE ?@E@@@^          J         RCY015            . YESX
)@@G@@S - JUMP DIGIT    @G@@@^          LA,U      A6,1              . SET FLAGSY
)@@G@@ FOR POSITIVE COUNT     @]@@@^RCY010    . @F@@@^          TG,U      A0,'SZ
)@@G@@0'            . MAKE SURE IT IS A DIGIT   @B@@@^          TG,U      A0,'TA
)@@G@@9'+1          .   @D@@@^          J         ERRCNT            . GUESS ITTB
)@@G@@ AINT @E@@@^          ANA,U     A0,'0'            . CONVERT TO BINARY   TC
)@@G@@@B@@@^          MSI,U     A2,10             .   @F@@@^          AA      TD
)@@G@@  A2,A0             . ADD IN TO RUNNING TOTAL   @]@@@^RCY015    . @F@@@^TE
)@@G@@          JZ        A1,RCY020         . IF NO MORE CHARS THEN EXIT@E@@@^TF
)@@G@@          LA,U      A0,0              . GET NEXT CHARACTER  @B@@@^      TG
)@@G@@    LDSL      A0,6              .   @D@@@^          TE,U      A0,' '    TH
)@@G@@        . IS IT BLANK ? @E@@@^          J         RCY010            . NOTI
)@@G@@ - LOOK AT IT     @]@@@^RCY020    . @D@@@^          TG,U      A2,29     TJ
)@@G@@        . IS IT INSANE ?@E@@@^          J         ERRCNT            . YETK
)@@G@@S - SAY SOMETHING @[@@@^.     @F@@@^          JZ        A2,$+2          TL
)@@G@@  . IF ZERO SIGN SHOULD BE +  @E@@@^          MSI       A2,A6           TM
)@@G@@  . TAKE ACCOUNT OF SIGN@E@@@^          S         A2,CYCOFF         . SETN
)@@G@@T CYCLE OFFSET    @[@@@^.     @[@@@^/.    @[@@@^.     @C@@@^. NOW PROCESTO
)@@G@@S THE HARDEST SPEC OF ALL (SPEC 1)  @[@@@^.     @E@@@^          LA,U    TP
)@@G@@  A0,1              . GET IT INTO ELT$    @D@@@^          CALL      SELTTQ
)@@G@@$             . USING INFOR$  @C@@@^          J         ERRFOR          TR
)@@G@@  . OOPS ?  @F@@@^          TNZ       FNL               . WAS THERE A FITS
)@@G@@LE NAME ?   @C@@@^          J         ERRFOR            . OOPS ?  @G@@@^TT
)@@G@@          DL        A0,DREADF         . GET USE NAME FOR CURRENT FCYCLE TU
)@@G@@@E@@@^          CALL      DUSE$             . DO DYNAMIC @USE     @C@@@^TV
)@@G@@          JNZ       A0,ERRFOR         . OOPS ?  @E@@@^          E$DIT   TW
)@@G@@  ED                . BUILD ASSIGN IMAGE  @B@@@^          E$COPY    6,('TX
)@@G@@@ASG,A')      .   @F@@@^          L,U       A0,'Y'            . IF NO ASTY
)@@G@@SIGN USE Y OPTION @F@@@^          TNZ       ASGOLD            . BUT IF ATZ

)@@G@@@E@@@[      SUBROUTINE PAKFIL (NSK,Q,F,FCS,FC,K1,K2,EC,ARR,NCOUNT)@[@@@[BQ
)@@G@@C     @ @@@[      IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  @A@@@[      DIMENSION Q(2), F(BR

)@@G@@@^@@@^      UNPK(13) = 1R*    @A[@@[      CALL UNPACK (12, F, UNPK(14)) BV
)@@G@@@C@]@[      IF (FCS .EQ. '-' .AND. FC .EQ. 0) GO TO 15@E@ @]      IF (FCBW
)@@G@@S .EQ. '-' .AND. FC .EQ. '     0') GO TO 15     @D@@@       IF (FCS .EQ.BX
)@@G@@ ' ' .AND. FC .EQ. ' ') GO TO 15    @ @^@[      UNPK(26) = '@@@@@('     BY
)@@G@@@^@@@^      UNPK(26) = 1R(    @ @]@[      UNPK(27) = FLD(0,6,FCS) @ @#@]BZ
)@@G@@      UNPK(27) = FLD(0,6,FC)  @ [@@#      UNPK(27) = FLD(0,6,FCS) @D@#@]CA

)@@G@@PK(27).EQ.5) UNPK(27) = FLD(18,6,FC)@D@@@^      IF (UNPK(27).EQ.1R ) UNPCC
)@@G@@K(27) = FLD(18,6,FC)    @#@]@[      I1 = FC/10  @^@]@[      I2 = FC-10*ICD
)@@G@@1     @ @]@[      I1 = I1 - 10*(I1/10)    @ @]@[      UNPK(28) = '@@@@@ CE
)@@G@@'     @ [@@]      UNPK(28) = FLD(24,6,FC) @B@]@[      IF (I1 .NE. 0) UNPCF
)@@G@@K(28) = I1+48     @^@]@[      UNPK(29) = I2+48  @ @@@]      UNPK(29) = FCG

)@@G@@'     @^@@@^20    UNPK(38) = 1R/    @A[@@[      CALL UNPACK (6, K2, UNPKCM
)@@G@@(39)) @ @@@[30    UNPK(45) = FLD(0,6,EC)  @A@^@[      CALL STRCON (NSK, CN
)@@G@@5, UNPK1)   @A@@@^      CALL STRCON (NSK, 1R , UNPK1) @#[@@[      I = NSCO
)@@G@@K+1   @^@@@[      DO 40 J = 1,45    @A@^@[      IF (UNPK(J) .EQ. 5) GO TCP

)@@G@@@^@@@4          E$CHAR    ' ' @ @@@4          E$TIME    TDATO     @#@@@4RX
)@@G@@          E$DITX  @B@@@4          L         A0,(PF 1,22,LINE)     @ @@@4RY
)@@G@@          ER        PRINT$    @[@@@4.     @ @@@4.         WRITE OUTPUT ERZ
)@@G@@LEMENT@[@@@4.     @G@@@4NOPRT     TEP       A13,(1*/('Z'-'W')) . W OPTIOSA
)@@G@@N SAYS WRITE IT ANYWAY  @B@@@4          J         WRITEIT           .   SB
)@@G@@@I@@@4          JNZ       A11,CORRUPTED     . IF FILE HAS BEEN CORRUPTEDSC
)@@G@@, TELL THE WOR    @I@@@4          JZ        A12,NOCHG         . OTHERWISSD
)@@G@@E, IF NO CHANGE - DONT WRITE IT     @]@@@4WRITEIT   . @H@@@4CHECKRETA* TSE
)@@G@@EP      A13,(1*/('Z'-'R')) . R OPTION SAYS DONT WRITE OUTPUT OMN  @ @@@4SF
)@@G@@          J         NOWRITE   @[@@@4.     @E@@@4. COMPUTE THE CHECKSUM FSG
)@@G@@OR THE OUTPUT OMN ELEMENT. SAVE THIS@D@@@4. INTERNAL CHECKSUM IN THE HEASH
)@@G@@DER OF THE ELEMENT.     @[@@@4.     @E@@@4          LA        A1,(1,FACISI
)@@G@@TO)     . READ THE HEADER     @F@@@4          LR,U      R1,28-1         SJ
)@@G@@  . WHICH IS 28 WORDS LONG    @G@@@4          SZ        A2              SK
)@@G@@  . CLEAR THE CHECKSUM ACCUMULATOR  @F@@@4          SSC       A2,1      SL
)@@G@@        . SHIFT THE ACCUMULATOR     @F@@@4          AA        A2,0,*A1  SM
)@@G@@        . ADD THE NECXT DATA WORD   @E@@@4          JGD       R1,$-2    SN
)@@G@@        . AND LOOP UNTIL DONE @F@@@4          IF NONZ,IN,FTYPEO OR ;    SO
)@@G@@  . TRACK BY TRACK CHECKSUM   @G@@@4          ZERO,IN,NELTSO THEN       SP
)@@G@@  . ******* REMOVE LATER *******    @G@@@4          LA        A1,FACITO+SQ
)@@G@@9,,H1   . LOAD MAX TRACK FROM FACIT$ PKT  @F@@@4          AA,U      A1,1SR
)@@G@@              . CONVERT TO # OF TRACKS    @F@@@4          ELSE          SS
)@@G@@              . WE ARE ELT BY ELT CHECKSUM@E@@@4          LA        A1,NST
)@@G@@ELTSO         . LOAD # OF ITEMS     @F@@@4          MSI,U     A1,7      SU
)@@G@@        . TIMES 7 TO GET WORD COUNT @E@@@4          ENDIF               SV
)@@G@@        . END OF FTYPE TEST   @H@@@4          LR        R1,A1           SW
)@@G@@  . LOAD THE ELEMENT TEXT LENGTH (WORDS)  @F@@@4          LA        A1,ASX
)@@G@@CWO+1,,H2     . ADDRESS OF ELEMENT TEXT   @B@@@4          LXI,U     A1,1SY
)@@G@@              .   @H@@@4          LR        R1,ACWO+1,,H1     . LOAD THESZ
)@@G@@ ELEMENT TEXT LENGTH (WORDS)  @F@@@4          J         $+3             TA
)@@G@@  . DECREMENT THE LOOP COUNTER@F@@@4          SSC       A2,1            TB
)@@G@@  . SHIFT THE ACCUMULATOR     @F@@@4          AA        A2,0,*A1        TC
)@@G@@  . ADD THE NECXT DATA WORD   @E@@@4          JGD       R1,$-2          TD
)@@G@@  . AND LOOP UNTIL DONE @H@@@4          SA        A2,CHKCHKO        . SATE
)@@G@@VE INTERNAL CHECKSUM IN HEADER.     @[@@@4.     @A@@@4.         WRITE OUTF
)@@G@@TPUT OMN ELEMENT  @[@@@4.     @H@@@4          L,H1      A0,ACWO+1       TG
)@@G@@  . LENGTH (WORDS) OF OUTPUT ELT TEXT     @E@@@4                        TH
)@@G@@              . EXCEPT FOR HEADER   @I@@@4          A,U       A0,27+28  TI
)@@G@@     . ROUND UPWARDS (27) + LENGTH OF HEADER (28).    @ @@@4          DSTJ
)@@G@@A       A0,36     @ @@@4          DI,U      A0,28     @B@@@4. GET A0 = LTK
)@@G@@ENGTH (SECTORS) OF OUTPUT ELT @F@@@4          AU        A0,PFWPKT+10    TL
)@@G@@  . GET NEW NEXTWRITE ADDRESS @D@@@4          S,H2      A0,PFWPKT+9     TM
)@@G@@  . SAVE LENGTH   @ @@@4          L,U       A0,OPKT   @^@@@4          ERTN
)@@G@@        IOW$@ @@@4          TZ,S1     OPKT+3    @E@@@4          ERROR   TO
)@@G@@  'IO ERROR WRITING SPEC 2 OUTPUT ELEMENT'@ @@@4          L,U       A0,PTP
)@@G@@FWPKT @ @@@4          ER        PFUWL$    @^@@@4          TZ        A2  TQ
)@@G@@@C@@@4          ERROR     'ERROR ON PFUWL$ - SPEC 2'  @ @@@4          L,TR

)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . OTHERWISE TELL THE WORLD WE INITTV
)@@G@@IALIZED     @ @@@4          E$MSG     INITMSG   @ @@@4          E$FD2   TW
